93: - ✅ `firestore.rules` (Firebase Firestore セキュリティルール) の本番デプロイが完了。

167: const toHiragana = (str) => {
168:   return str.replace(/[\u30a1-\u30f6]/g, (match) => {
169:     return String.fromCharCode(match.charCodeAt(0) - 0x60);
170:   });
171: };
172: 
173: function generateAllRomaji(text) {
174:   const normalized = toHiragana(text);
175:   const results = [];
176:   
177:   function recurse(index, currentRomaji) {
178:     if (index >= normalized.length) {
179:       results.push(currentRomaji);
180:       return;
181:     }
182:     
183:     // 促音「っ」の処理
184:     if (normalized[index] === 'っ') {
185:       if (index + 1 < normalized.length) {
186:         let nextChar2 = normalized.substring(index + 1, index + 3);
187:         let nextChar1 = normalized[index + 1];
188:         
189:         let nextRomajis = [];
190:         let consumed = 0;
191:         
192:         if (ROMAJI_TABLE[nextChar2]) {
193:           nextRomajis = ROMAJI_TABLE[nextChar2];
194:           consumed = 2;
195:         } else if (ROMAJI_TABLE[nextChar1]) {
196:           nextRomajis = ROMAJI_TABLE[nextChar1];
197:           consumed = 1;
198:         }
199:         
200:         if (nextRomajis.length > 0) {
201:           nextRomajis.forEach(r => {
202:             const firstChar = r[0];
203:             recurse(index + 1 + consumed, currentRomaji + firstChar + r);
204:           });
205:           return;
206:         }
207:       }
208:       recurse(index + 1, currentRomaji + 'tsu');
209:       return;
210:     }
211:     
212:     // 2文字のチェック
213:     if (index + 1 < normalized.length) {
214:       const char2 = normalized.substring(index, index + 2);
215:       if (ROMAJI_TABLE[char2]) {
216:         ROMAJI_TABLE[char2].forEach(r => {
217:           recurse(index + 2, currentRomaji + r);
218:         });
219:         return;
220:       }
221:     }
222:     
223:     // 1文字のチェック
224:     const char1 = normalized[index];
225:     if (ROMAJI_TABLE[char1]) {
226:       ROMAJI_TABLE[char1].forEach(r => {
227:         recurse(index + 1, currentRomaji + r);
228:       });
229:     } else {
230:       recurse(index + 1, currentRomaji + char1.toLowerCase());
231:     }
232:   }
233:   
234:   recurse(0, '');
235:   return [...new Set(results)];
236: }

586: // 難易度自動判定ロジック
587: const hasSymbolOrNumber = (text) => {
588:   return /[！？!?。、,.\d０-９]/.test(text);
589: };
590: 
591: const determineDifficulty = (word) => {
592:   const len = word.length;
593:   if (hasSymbolOrNumber(word)) {
594:     return 'ベリーハード';
595:   } else if (len === 2) {
596:     return 'イージー';
597:   } else if (len >= 3 && len <= 5) {
598:     return 'ノーマル';
599:   } else {
600:     return 'ハード';
601:   }
602: };

1391:                   currentPlayers[existingPlayerIndex].isCloudSync = true;

1393:                   playersChanged = true;
1394:                 }
1395:               } else {
1396:                 // ローカルの方が新しい、または同じ場合は上書きせず、isCloudSync を false にしてクラウドへのアップロード待ちにする

7065:                     <div className="text-base mt-1">ガチャチケット</div>
7066:                   </div>
7067:                 ) : ticketReward.type === 'bgm' ? (
7068:                   <div className="w-48 py-8 rounded-2xl bg-gradient-to-r from-emerald-500 to-teal-500 border-4 border-yellow-300 text-white font-black text-center shadow-lg transform rotate-3 hover:rotate-0 transition-transform duration-300 relative overflow-hidden">
7069:                     <div className="text-5xl mb-2 animate-bounce">🎵💿🎵</div>
7070:                     <div className="text-xs tracking-wider">おんがくの</div>
7071:                     <div className="text-base mt-1">ガチャチケット</div>
7072:                   </div>
7073:                 ) : (
7074:                   <div className="w-48 py-8 rounded-2xl bg-gradient-to-r from-yellow-400 to-amber-500 border-4 border-yellow-300 text-white font-black text-center shadow-lg transform -rotate-3 hover:rotate-0 transition-transform duration-300 relative overflow-hidden">
7075:                     <div className="text-5xl mb-2 animate-bounce">🎨🎟️🎨</div>
7076:                     <div className="text-xs tracking-wider">はいけいの</div>
7077:                     <div className="text-base mt-1">ガチャチケット</div>
7078:                   </div>
7079:                 )}
7080:               </div>
7081:               
7082:               <p className="text-base font-black text-gray-700 leading-snug">
7083:                 {ticketReward.type === 'legend' 
7084:                   ? '🌟 激レア以上確定チケット 🌟' 
7085:                   : ticketReward.type === 'se'
7086:                   ? '🔊 こうかおんガチャチケット 🔊'
7087:                   : ticketReward.type === 'bgm'
7088:                   ? '🎵 おんがくガチャチケット 🎵'
7089:                   : '🎨 はいけいガチャチケット 🎨'}
7090:                 <br />
7091:                 を {ticketReward.count || 1}まい ゲットしたよ！
7092:               </p>
7093:               
7094:               <button
7095:                 onClick={() => {
7096:                   const onConfirm = ticketReward.onConfirm;
7097:                   setTicketReward(null);
7098:                   if (onConfirm) onConfirm();
7099:                 }}
7100:                 className="premium-button bg-gradient-to-r from-yellow-400 to-orange-500 hover:from-yellow-500 hover:to-orange-600 text-white font-black text-lg px-8 py-3 w-full shadow-lg"
7101:               >
7102:                 {ticketReward.titleObj ? 'やったー！' : 'つぎへすすむ'}
7103:               </button>
7104:             </div>
7105:           </div>
7106:         </div>
7107:       )}
7108: 
7109:     {/* 初回同期ローディング */}
7110:     {isSyncing && (
7111:       <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-sky-500 z-[100] flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-4">
7112:         <div className="text-white text-5xl mb-4 animate-bounce">☁️</div>
7113:         <h2 className="text-white text-xl md:text-2xl font-black mb-2">データをよみこみ中...</h2>
7114:         <div className="w-48 h-2 bg-sky-400 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
7115:           <div className="w-1/2 h-full bg-white animate-pulse" />
7116:         </div>
7117:       </div>
7118:     )}
7119: 
7120: 
7121: 
7122:       {/* 画面右下のセーブ中インジケータ */}
7123:       {isSaving && (
7124:         <div className="fixed bottom-4 right-4 z-[9999] flex items-center gap-2 bg-white/80 dark:bg-gray-800/80 backdrop-blur-md px-3.5 py-2 rounded-full shadow-lg border border-white/20 text-xs font-black text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-200 animate-fade-in pointer-events-none">
7125:           <RefreshCcw className="w-3.5 h-3.5 animate-spin text-green-500" />
7126:           <span>セーブ中...</span>
7127:         </div>
7128:       )}
7129: 
7130:     </div>
7131:   );
7132: }
